It is up\n     to the hook to use what it needs.  */\n  void (* early_global_decl) (tree decl);\n\n  /* Augment debug information generated by early_global_decl with\n     more complete debug info (if applicable).  Called from toplev.cc\n     after the compilation proper has finished and cgraph information\n     is available.\n\n     This gets called for both variables and functions.\n\n     Location information is usually available at this point, unless\n     the hook is being called for a decl that has been optimized away.\n\n     This hook may be called on VAR_DECLs or FUNCTION_DECLs. Chain\\n\\nGCC's DWARF debug information generation follows a well-structured pipeline from front-end declarations through final assembly output:\\n\\n### Debug Hooks Interface\\nThe foundation is the `gcc_debug_hooks` structure defined in **gcc/debug.h**, which provides callback hooks that the front-end compiler calls at various compilation stages. The **gcc/debug.cc** file provides default no-op implementations. The DWARF-specific hooks are defined as `dwarf2_debug_hooks` in **gcc/dwarf2out.cc** (line 2893), which registers DWARF-specific callback functions.\\n\\n### DIE (Debug Info Entry) Creation\\nThe core data structure for DWARF is the `die_struct` defined in **gcc/dwarf2out.cc** (line 3146), which represents individual debug information entries. This structure contains:\\n- Attributes (die_attr) stored as vectors of dw_attr_node\\n- Parent/child/sibling pointers for tree structure\\n- A tag identifying the DIE type (function, variable, type, etc.)\\n- Abbreviation and offset information\\n\\nDIE instances are created via:\\n- `new_die_raw()` (line 5850) - allocates a bare DIE\\n- `new_die()` (line 5863) - creates a DIE with parent linkage\\n- `add_child_die()` (line 5771) - establishes parent-child relationships\\n\\nDIE attributes are added via numerous `add_AT_*` functions (add_AT_flag, add_AT_int, add_AT_unsigned, add_AT_string, add_AT_die_ref, add_AT_loc, add_AT_loc_list, etc.) that populate the `dw_val_node` structures.\\n\\n### Front-End Hook Entry Points\\nThe debug hooks connect the front-end to DWARF generation:\\n1. **dwarf2out_early_global_decl()** (line 27788) - Called early after declaration parsing for functions, variables, and types\\n2. **dwarf2out_late_global_decl()** (line 27883) - Called later with complete location information\\n3. **dwarf2out_function_decl()** (line 28239) - Called for function declarations with full body information\\n\\nThese hooks invoke **dwarf2out_decl()** (line 28146), which dispatches to **gen_decl_die()** (line 27537) based on declaration type (FUNCTION_DECL, VAR_DECL, TYPE_DECL, etc.).\\n\\n### Declaration and Type DIE Generation\\n**gen_decl_die()** orchestrates creation of DIEs for different declaration types:\\n- Functions: calls **gen_subprogram_die()** (line 23937) to create DW_TAG_subprogram DIEs\\n- Types: calls **gen_type_die()** (line 27004) and **gen_type_die_with_usage()** (line 26764)\\n- Types within classes: **gen_type_die_for_member()** (line 23634)\\n- Constants: **gen_const_die()**\\n\\n### Line Number Recording\\nThe debug hook **dwarf2out_source_line()** (line 29183) is called by the back-end during code generation to record source location information. This function:\\n- Records file number via **lookup_filename()** and **maybe_emit_file()**\\n- Updates the current line info table with line, column, and discriminator information\\n- Emits .loc directives for assembly-level line information\\n\\nLine numbers are accumulated in `dw_line_info_table` structures during compilation and output later.\\n\\n### Line Number Table Emission\\nThe **output_line_info()** function (line 13137) generates the complete .debug_line section:\\n1. Outputs DWARF line number header information (version, opcode base, line range, etc.)\\n2. Calls **output_file_names()** (line 12599) to output the file table\\n3. For each line info table, calls **output_one_line_info_table()** (line 12982) to emit line number sequences\\n4. Generates line number program instructions encoding the mapping between addresses and source lines\\n\\n### Final Output Generation\\n**dwarf2out_finish()** (line 32814) orchestrates the complete DWARF output generation:\\n1. Flushes remaining DIEs from the limbo list\\n2. Resolves addresses and relocations\\n3. Adds sibling attributes to DIEs\\n4. Calls **output_die()** (line 10830) and **output_die_abbrevs()** (line 10203) to emit all DIE data\\n5. Calls **output_line_info()** to emit the line number table\\n6. Outputs frame information via dwarf2cfi.cc for exception handling and unwinding\\n\\n### Assembly Output Helpers\\n**gcc/dwarf2asm.cc** provides low-level assembly output helpers:\\n- **dw2_assemble_integer()** and related dw2_asm_output_* functions encode DWARF data into assembly directives\\n- These functions handle relocations, address sizing, and encoding according to the target architecture\\n\\n### Integration Points\\n- The type definitions in **gcc/dwarf2out.h** define the data structures used throughout\\n- **gcc/dwarf2cfi.cc** handles Call Frame Information (CFI) and exception handling metadata\\n- The debug hooks in debug.h provide the interface allowing any debug format (not just DWARF) to be plugged in\\n\\nThis architecture enables GCC to generate comprehensive DWARF debug information while remaining modular and supporting multiple debug output formats through the hook interface.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":4,"cache_creation_input_tokens":767,"cache_read_input_tokens":63124,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":767},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"80345433-fe69-4e07-b174-b6b8de3b5fa2","uuid":"c90e927b-0c7f-4881-882a-ea378e315ccb"}

Chain\\n\\nGCC's DWARF debug information generation follows a well-structured pipeline from front-end declarations through final assembly output:\\n\\n### Debug Hooks Interface\\nThe foundation is the `gcc_debug_hooks` structure defined in **gcc/debug.h**, which provides callback hooks that the front-end compiler calls at various compilation stages. The **gcc/debug.cc** file provides default no-op implementations. The DWARF-specific hooks are defined as `dwarf2_debug_hooks` in **gcc/dwarf2out.cc** (line 2893), which registers DWARF-specific callback functions.\\n\\n### DIE (Debug Info Entry) Creation\\nThe core data structure for DWARF is the `die_struct` defined in **gcc/dwarf2out.cc** (line 3146), which represents individual debug information entries. This structure contains:\\n- Attributes (die_attr) stored as vectors of dw_attr_node\\n- Parent/child/sibling pointers for tree structure\\n- A tag identifying the DIE type (function, variable, type, etc.)\\n- Abbreviation and offset information\\n\\nDIE instances are created via:\\n- `new_die_raw()` (line 5850) - allocates a bare DIE\\n- `new_die()` (line 5863) - creates a DIE with parent linkage\\n- `add_child_die()` (line 5771) - establishes parent-child relationships\\n\\nDIE attributes are added via numerous `add_AT_*` functions (add_AT_flag, add_AT_int, add_AT_unsigned, add_AT_string, add_AT_die_ref, add_AT_loc, add_AT_loc_list, etc.) that populate the `dw_val_node` structures.\\n\\n### Front-End Hook Entry Points\\nThe debug hooks connect the front-end to DWARF generation:\\n1. **dwarf2out_early_global_decl()** (line 27788) - Called early after declaration parsing for functions, variables, and types\\n2. **dwarf2out_late_global_decl()** (line 27883) - Called later with complete location information\\n3. **dwarf2out_function_decl()** (line 28239) - Called for function declarations with full body information\\n\\nThese hooks invoke **dwarf2out_decl()** (line 28146), which dispatches to **gen_decl_die()** (line 27537) based on declaration type (FUNCTION_DECL, VAR_DECL, TYPE_DECL, etc.).\\n\\n### Declaration and Type DIE Generation\\n**gen_decl_die()** orchestrates creation of DIEs for different declaration types:\\n- Functions: calls **gen_subprogram_die()** (line 23937) to create DW_TAG_subprogram DIEs\\n- Types: calls **gen_type_die()** (line 27004) and **gen_type_die_with_usage()** (line 26764)\\n- Types within classes: **gen_type_die_for_member()** (line 23634)\\n- Constants: **gen_const_die()**\\n\\n### Line Number Recording\\nThe debug hook **dwarf2out_source_line()** (line 29183) is called by the back-end during code generation to record source location information. This function:\\n- Records file number via **lookup_filename()** and **maybe_emit_file()**\\n- Updates the current line info table with line, column, and discriminator information\\n- Emits .loc directives for assembly-level line information\\n\\nLine numbers are accumulated in `dw_line_info_table` structures during compilation and output later.\\n\\n### Line Number Table Emission\\nThe **output_line_info()** function (line 13137) generates the complete .debug_line section:\\n1. Outputs DWARF line number header information (version, opcode base, line range, etc.)\\n2. Calls **output_file_names()** (line 12599) to output the file table\\n3. For each line info table, calls **output_one_line_info_table()** (line 12982) to emit line number sequences\\n4. Generates line number program instructions encoding the mapping between addresses and source lines\\n\\n### Final Output Generation\\n**dwarf2out_finish()** (line 32814) orchestrates the complete DWARF output generation:\\n1. Flushes remaining DIEs from the limbo list\\n2. Resolves addresses and relocations\\n3. Adds sibling attributes to DIEs\\n4. Calls **output_die()** (line 10830) and **output_die_abbrevs()** (line 10203) to emit all DIE data\\n5. Calls **output_line_info()** to emit the line number table\\n6. Outputs frame information via dwarf2cfi.cc for exception handling and unwinding\\n\\n### Assembly Output Helpers\\n**gcc/dwarf2asm.cc** provides low-level assembly output helpers:\\n- **dw2_assemble_integer()** and related dw2_asm_output_* functions encode DWARF data into assembly directives\\n- These functions handle relocations, address sizing, and encoding according to the target architecture\\n\\n### Integration Points\\n- The type definitions in **gcc/dwarf2out.h** define the data structures used throughout\\n- **gcc/dwarf2cfi.cc** handles Call Frame Information (CFI) and exception handling metadata\\n- The debug hooks in debug.h provide the interface allowing any debug format (not just DWARF) to be plugged in\\n\\nThis architecture enables GCC to generate comprehensive DWARF debug information while remaining modular and supporting multiple debug output formats through the hook interface.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
